\u003cem\u003eAsk questions, share what you've built, get help from the community.\u003c/em\u003e\n\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eYou just joined a new team. The codebase is 200,000 lines of code. Where do you even start?\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eUnderstand Anything is a \u003ca href=\"https://code.claude.com/docs/en/plugins-reference#plugins-reference\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eClaude Code Plugin\u003c/a\u003e that analyzes your project with a multi-agent pipeline, builds a knowledge graph of every file, function, class, and dependency, then gives you an interactive dashboard to explore it all visually. 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eStatic analysis and LLMs do what each does best:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTree-sitter (deterministic)\u003c/strong\u003e — parses source into a concrete syntax tree and extracts structural facts: imports, exports, function/class definitions, call sites, inheritance. Pre-resolved into an \u003ccode\u003eimportMap\u003c/code\u003e during the scan phase and passed to file-analyzers so they don't re-derive imports from source. Same input → same output, every run. Also powers fingerprint-based change detection for incremental updates.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLLM (semantic)\u003c/strong\u003e — reads the parsed structure alongside the original source to produce what parsers can't: plain-English summaries, tags, architectural layer assignments, business-domain mapping, guided tours, language concept callouts.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis split is why the graph is reproducible on the structural side (the same code always yields the same edges) while still capturing intent on the semantic side (what a file is \u003cem\u003efor\u003c/em\u003e, not just what it imports).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eMulti-Agent Pipeline\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-multi-agent-pipeline\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Multi-Agent Pipeline\" href=\"#multi-agent-pipeline\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe \u003ccode\u003e/understand\u003c/code\u003e command orchestrates 5 specialized agents, and \u003ccode\u003e/understand-domain\u003c/code\u003e adds a 6th:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eAgent\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eRole\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003eproject-scanner\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eDiscover files, detect languages and frameworks\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003efile-analyzer\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eExtract functions, classes, imports; produce graph nodes and edges\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003earchitecture-analyzer\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eIdentify architectural layers\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003etour-builder\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eGenerate guided learning tours\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003egraph-reviewer\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eValidate graph completeness and referential integrity (runs inline by default; use \u003ccode\u003e--review\u003c/code\u003e for full LLM review)\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003edomain-analyzer\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eExtract business domains, flows, and process steps (used by \u003ccode\u003e/understand-domain\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003earticle-analyzer\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eExtract entities, claims, and implicit relationships from wiki articles (used by \u003ccode\u003e/understand-knowledge\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\u003c/markdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFile analyzers run in parallel (up to 5 concurrent, 20-30 files per batch). Supports incremental updates — only re-analyzes files that changed since the last run.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\"   <strong>Turn any codebase, knowledge base, or docs into an interactive knowledge graph you can explore, search, and ask questions about.</strong>

<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Lum1104/Understand-Anything/blob/main/assets/hero.png"><img src="/Lum1104/Understand-Anything/raw/main/assets/hero.png" alt="Understand Anything — Turn any codebase into an interactive knowledge graph" width="800" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</p>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <strong>💬 <a href="https://discord.gg/pydat66RY" rel="nofollow">Join the Discord community →</a></strong>
  <br>
  <em>Ask questions, share what you've built, get help from the community.</em>
</p>
<hr>
<p dir="auto"><strong>You just joined a new team. The codebase is 200,000 lines of code. Where do you even start?</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Understand Anything is a <a href="https://code.claude.com/docs/en/plugins-reference#plugins-reference" rel="nofollow">Claude Code Plugin</a> that analyzes your project with a multi-agent pipeline, builds a knowledge graph of every file, function, class, and dependency, then gives you an interactive dashboard to explore it all visually. Stop reading code blind. Start seeing the big picture.</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>The goal isn't a graph that wows you with how complex your codebase is — it's a graph that quietly teaches you how every piece fits together.</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">✨ Features</h2><a id="user-content--features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ✨ Features" href="#-features"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p><p dir="auto"><strong>Want to skip the reading?</strong> Try the <a href="https://understand-anything.com/demo/" rel="nofollow">live demo</a> in our <a href="https://understand-anything.com/" rel="nofollow">homepage</a> — a fully interactive dashboard you can pan, zoom, search, and explore right in your browser.</p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Explore the structural graph</h3><a id="user-content-explore-the-structural-graph" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Explore the structural graph" href="#explore-the-structural-graph"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Navigate your codebase as an interactive knowledge graph — every file, function, and class is a node you can click, search, and explore. Select any node to see plain-English summaries, relationships, and guided tours.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Understand business logic</h3><a id="user-content-understand-business-logic" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Understand business logic" href="#understand-business-logic"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Switch to the domain view and see how your code maps to real business processes — domains, flows, and steps laid out as a horizontal graph.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Analyze knowledge bases</h3><a id="user-content-analyze-knowledge-bases" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Analyze knowledge bases" href="#analyze-knowledge-bases"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Point <code>/understand-knowledge</code> at a <a href="https://gist.github.com/karpathy/442a6bf555914893e9891c11519de94f">Karpathy-pattern LLM wiki</a> and get a force-directed knowledge graph with community clustering. The deterministic parser extracts wikilinks and categories from <code>index.md</code>, then LLM agents discover implicit relationships, extract entities, and surface claims — turning your wiki into a navigable graph of interconnected ideas.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Analyze your codebase</h3><a id="user-content-2-analyze-your-codebase" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Analyze your codebase" href="#2-analyze-your-codebase"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/understand"><pre>/understand</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">A multi-agent pipeline scans your project, extracts every file, function, class, and dependency, then builds a knowledge graph saved to <code>.understand-anything/knowledge-graph.json</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Localized output:</strong> Use <code>--language</code> to generate content in your preferred language:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Generate Chinese content (知识图节点描述和 Dashboard UI)
/understand --language zh

# Supported languages: en (default), zh, zh-TW, ja, ko, ru"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Generate Chinese content (知识图节点描述和 Dashboard UI)</span>
/understand --language zh

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Supported languages: en (default), zh, zh-TW, ja, ko, ru</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>--language</code> parameter affects:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Node summaries and descriptions in the knowledge graph</li>
<li>Dashboard UI labels, buttons, and tooltips</li>
<li>Guided tour explanations</li>
</ul>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/understand-dashboard"><pre>/understand-dashboard</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">An interactive web dashboard opens with your codebase visualized as a graph — color-coded by architectural layer, searchable, and clickable. Select any node to see its code, relationships, and a plain-English explanation.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. Keep learning</h3><a id="user-content-4-keep-learning" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. Keep learning" href="#4-keep-learning"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Ask anything about the codebase
/understand-chat How does the payment flow work?

# Analyze impact of your current changes
/understand-diff

# Deep-dive into a specific file or function
/understand-explain src/auth/login.ts

# Generate an onboarding guide for new team members
/understand-onboard

# Extract business domain knowledge (domains, flows, steps)
/understand-domain

# Analyze a Karpathy-pattern LLM wiki knowledge base
/understand-knowledge ~/path/to/wiki

# Re-run anytime — incremental by default (only re-analyzes changed files)
/understand

# Auto-update on every commit via a post-commit hook
/understand --auto-update

# Scope to a subdirectory (for huge monorepos)
/understand src/frontend"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Ask anything about the codebase</span>
/understand-chat How does the payment flow work<span class="pl-k">?</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Analyze impact of your current changes</span>
/understand-diff

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Deep-dive into a specific file or function</span>
/understand-explain src/auth/login.ts

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Generate an onboarding guide for new team members</span>
/understand-onboard

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Extract business domain knowledge (domains, flows, steps)</span>
/understand-domain

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Analyze a Karpathy-pattern LLM wiki knowledge base</span>
/understand-knowledge <span class="pl-k">~</span>/path/to/wiki

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Re-run anytime — incremental by default (only re-analyzes changed files)</span>
/understand

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Auto-update on every commit via a post-commit hook</span>
/understand --auto-update

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Scope to a subdirectory (for huge monorepos)</span>
/understand src/frontend</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">One-line install (Codex / OpenCode / OpenClaw / Antigravity / Gemini CLI / Pi Agent / Vibe CLI / VS Code Copilot / Hermes / Cline / KIMI CLI)</h3><a id="user-content-one-line-install-codex--opencode--openclaw--antigravity--gemini-cli--pi-agent--vibe-cli--vs-code-copilot--hermes--cline--kimi-cli" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: One-line install (Codex / OpenCode / OpenClaw / Antigravity / Gemini CLI / Pi Agent / Vibe CLI / VS Code Copilot / Hermes / Cline / KIMI CLI)" href="#one-line-install-codex--opencode--openclaw--antigravity--gemini-cli--pi-agent--vibe-cli--vs-code-copilot--hermes--cline--kimi-cli"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>macOS / Linux:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Lum1104/Understand-Anything/main/install.sh | bash
# or skip the prompt by passing the platform:
curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Lum1104/Understand-Anything/main/install.sh | bash -s codex"><pre>curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Lum1104/Understand-Anything/main/install.sh <span class="pl-k">|</span> bash
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> or skip the prompt by passing the platform:</span>
curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Lum1104/Understand-Anything/main/install.sh <span class="pl-k">|</span> bash -s codex</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Windows (PowerShell):</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="iwr -useb https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Lum1104/Understand-Anything/main/install.ps1 | iex"><pre>iwr <span class="pl-k">-</span>useb https:<span class="pl-k">//</span><span class="pl-c1">raw.githubusercontent.com</span><span class="pl-k">/</span>Lum1104<span class="pl-k">/</span>Understand<span class="pl-k">-</span>Anything<span class="pl-k">/</span>main<span class="pl-k">/</span>install.ps1 <span class="pl-k">|</span> iex</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The installer clones the repo to <code>~/.understand-anything/repo</code> and creates the right symlinks for the chosen platform. Restart your CLI/IDE afterwards.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Supported <code>&lt;platform&gt;</code> values: <code>gemini</code>, <code>codex</code>, <code>opencode</code>, <code>pi</code>, <code>openclaw</code>, <code>antigravity</code>, <code>vibe</code>, <code>vscode</code>, <code>hermes</code>, <code>cline</code>, <code>kimi</code></li>
<li>Update later: <code>./install.sh --update</code></li>
<li>Uninstall: <code>./install.sh --uninstall &lt;platform&gt;</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Cursor</h3><a id="user-content-cursor" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Cursor" href="#cursor"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Cursor auto-discovers the plugin via <code>.cursor-plugin/plugin.json</code> when this repo is cloned. No manual installation needed — just clone and open in Cursor.</p>
<p dir="auto">If auto-discovery doesn't pick it up, install it manually: open <strong>Cursor Settings → Plugins</strong>, paste <code>https://github.com/Lum1104/Understand-Anything</code> into the search field, and add it from there.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">VS Code + GitHub Copilot</h3><a id="user-content-vs-code--github-copilot" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: VS Code + GitHub Copilot" href="#vs-code--github-copilot"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">VS Code with GitHub Copilot (v1.108+) auto-discovers the plugin via <code>.copilot-plugin/plugin.json</code> when this repo is cloned. No manual installation needed — just clone and open in VS Code.</p>
<p dir="auto">For personal skills (available across all projects), run the <code>install.sh</code> above with the <code>vscode</code> platform.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Copilot CLI</h3><a id="user-content-copilot-cli" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Copilot CLI" href="#copilot-cli"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Platform Compatibility</h3><a id="user-content-platform-compatibility" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Platform Compatibility" href="#platform-compatibility"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📦 Share the Graph with Your Team</h2><a id="user-content--share-the-graph-with-your-team" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📦 Share the Graph with Your Team" href="#-share-the-graph-with-your-team"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The graph is just JSON — <strong>commit it once, and teammates skip the pipeline</strong>. Good for onboarding, PR reviews, and docs-as-code.</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example:</strong> <a href="https://github.com/Lum1104/microservices-demo">GoogleCloudPlatform/microservices-demo (fork)</a> — Go / Java / Python / Node reference with a committed graph.</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>What to commit:</strong> everything in <code>.understand-anything/</code> <em>except</em> <code>intermediate/</code> and <code>diff-overlay.json</code> (those are local scratch).</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-gitignore notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=".understand-anything/intermediate/
.understand-anything/diff-overlay.json"><pre><span class="pl-e">.understand-anything</span>/<span class="pl-e">intermediate</span>/
<span class="pl-e">.understand-anything</span>/<span class="pl-e">diff-overlay.json</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Keep it fresh:</strong> enable <code>/understand --auto-update</code> — a post-commit hook incrementally patches the graph so each commit lands with a matching graph. Or re-run <code>/understand</code> manually before releases.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Large graphs (10 MB+):</strong> track with <strong>git-lfs</strong>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="git lfs install
git lfs track &quot;.understand-anything/*.json&quot;
git add .gitattributes .understand-anything/"><pre>git lfs install
git lfs track <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>.understand-anything/*.json<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
git add .gitattributes .understand-anything/</pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔧 Under the Hood</h2><a id="user-content--under-the-hood" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔧 Under the Hood" href="#-under-the-hood"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tree-sitter + LLM hybrid</h3><a id="user-content-tree-sitter--llm-hybrid" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tree-sitter + LLM hybrid" href="#tree-sitter--llm-hybrid"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Static analysis and LLMs do what each does best:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Tree-sitter (deterministic)</strong> — parses source into a concrete syntax tree and extracts structural facts: imports, exports, function/class definitions, call sites, inheritance. Pre-resolved into an <code>importMap</code> during the scan phase and passed to file-analyzers so they don't re-derive imports from source. Same input → same output, every run. Also powers fingerprint-based change detection for incremental updates.</li>
<li><strong>LLM (semantic)</strong> — reads the parsed structure alongside the original source to produce what parsers can't: plain-English summaries, tags, architectural layer assignments, business-domain mapping, guided tours, language concept callouts.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">This split is why the graph is reproducible on the structural side (the same code always yields the same edges) while still capturing intent on the semantic side (what a file is <em>for</em>, not just what it imports).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Multi-Agent Pipeline</h3><a id="user-content-multi-agent-pipeline" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Multi-Agent Pipeline" href="#multi-agent-pipeline"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>/understand</code> command orchestrates 5 specialized agents, and <code>/understand-domain</code> adds a 6th:</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Agent</th>
<th>Role</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>project-scanner</code></td>
<td>Discover files, detect languages and frameworks</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>file-analyzer</code></td>
<td>Extract functions, classes, imports; produce graph nodes and edges</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>architecture-analyzer</code></td>
<td>Identify architectural layers</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>tour-builder</code></td>
<td>Generate guided learning tours</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>graph-reviewer</code></td>
<td>Validate graph completeness and referential integrity (runs inline by default; use <code>--review</code> for full LLM review)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>domain-analyzer</code></td>
<td>Extract business domains, flows, and process steps (used by <code>/understand-domain</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>article-analyzer</code></td>
<td>Extract entities, claims, and implicit relationships from wiki articles (used by <code>/understand-knowledge</code>)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto">File analyzers run in parallel (up to 5 concurrent, 20-30 files per batch). Supports incremental updates — only re-analyzes files that changed since the last run.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎥 Community</h2><a id="user-content--community" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎥 Community" href="#-community"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VmIUXVlt7_I" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/83110e67e7cfc1d6c6a16e67fb3014d3a9e421963627cdc68f45952b016afd62/68747470733a2f2f696d672e796f75747562652e636f6d2f76692f566d495558566c74375f492f6d617872657364656661756c742e6a7067" alt="Community walkthrough by Better Stack — watch on YouTube" width="480" data-canonical-src="https://img.youtube.com/vi/VmIUXVlt7_I/maxresdefault.jpg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🤝 Contributing</h2><a id="user-content--contributing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🤝 Contributing" href="#-contributing"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Contributions are welcome! Here's how to get started:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Fork the repository</li>
<li>Create a feature branch (<code>git checkout -b feature/my-feature</code>)</li>
<li>Run the tests (<code>pnpm --filter @understand-anything/core test</code>)</li>
<li>Commit your changes and open a pull request</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Please open an issue first for major changes so we can discuss the approach.</p>
<hr>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <strong>Stop reading code blind. Start understanding everything.</strong>
</p>

  <h2 class="tmp-mb-3 h4">About</h2>

      <p class="f4 tmp-my-3">
        Graphs that teach &gt; graphs that impress. Turn any code into an interactive knowledge graph you can explore, search, and ask questions about. Works with Claude Code, Codex, Cursor, Copilot, Gemini CLI, and more.
      </p>
      <div class="tmp-my-3 d-flex flex-items-center">
        <svg aria-hidden="true" data-component="Octicon" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-link flex-shrink-0 mr-2 tmp-mr-2">
    <path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path>
</svg>
        <span class="flex-auto min-width-0 css-truncate css-truncate-target width-fit">
          <a title="https://understand-anything.com" role="link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" class="text-bold" href="https://understand-anything.com">understand-anything.com</a>
        </span>
      </div>
